< review>
Best place to get Disney treats without going in the park! This is the place to get Churro Toffee, homemade caramel apples and yes you can watch the talented castmembers make them! So many treats to choose from so don't miss this sweet place! Once you are inside take a number if you would like to purchase anything in the glass display areas and they will help you out. Items purchased from the shelf can be purchased at the register like normal< /review>

Mar Vy< /user_name>
<response>None</response><rating>3< /rating><Review>There were so many sweets, such as, chocolates, English Toffee, Chocolate Dipped Pretzel, Mickey Chocolate Truffle, colorful Jelly Beans, Popcorn, Cookies, Cake Pops, fudge, and Chocolate Covered Strawberries, etc. They also make creative candy apples and some look like Disney characters.  I bought the Chocolate Caramel Popcorn , Cake Pop , three Chocolate Covered Strawberries, and one Candy Apple Peanut Caramel

~Sweets~
Another favorite dessert that I love are the Chocolate Covered Strawberries. I bought three, milk chocolate with dark chocolate swirls, white chocolate with milk chocolate swirls, and milk chocolate sprinkled with dark chocolate  chips. Even if the strawberries were a little tart, the chocolate was rich and smooth; it was delicious.  The Candy Apple Peanut Caramel was perfectly coated with gooey caramel, crunchy peanuts and the apple was crisp. Next is the Chocolate Carmel Popcorn that tasted fresh and surprisingly not very sweet.  My daughter wanted  the Cake Pop, the cake was soft and the ears were made of marshmallows.

~Customer Service~
Based on what I bought I would rate this place four stars but I lowered it to three because the friendly attitude from the staff could be better.

~Notes~
If you have an annual pass you will receive a discount.<//Review>< Pictures>

<Pictures>None< /Pictures><rate>4< /rate><Gmap_id>0x80dcd7d09ab6a573:0xa0d021689e0265b4< /Gmap_id><user_name>Stephanie V< /user_name>< time>
1525585918886< /time>
< text>
Based on Walt Disney's hometown of Marceline, Missouri, this small confectionery shop offers delicious pastries and sweet treats to indulge while on a visit to the Disneyland Resort.

They have a nice selection of sweets and candy apples. They have cookies, fudge, cupcakes, cake pops, chocolate covered strawberries, etc. I'm not sure where else they offer it, but they have a pineapple slice dipped in dark chocolate and it's so good! Must try! They also have a delicious white chocolate raspberry cookie. Tons of guest stop by to observe and admire the cast members working on the candy apples. They have such cute designs, especially closer to Halloween and the holidays.

They also have some items already boxed up and ready for purchase such as cookies, candy, and teas. They have a small selection of mugs and kitchen items, but for more variety I would head over to World of Disney.<//text>

< Review>
Everything has been great for me.

I've been to this office before and didn't have the bad experience conveyed by others. So I wanted to give them another chance.

Before I start, I'm not denying anyone else's experience and the bad reviews here. I'm just conveying my experience which happens to be different. Take that as you will.

But as to "no more walk-ins", that's completely incorrect. The phone line for Quest says "walk-ins are always welcome". I called for an appointment but it said the earliest available slot was in two days. I already fasted for a blood test so I just went in. There is a sign-in sheet for appointments and walk-ins. Hardly anyone was there (Wednesday AM). I got in with no problem.

I was told that on Saturdays they get a lot of people with appointments and the walk-ins fill up the rest of the schedule early in the morning. That's basic "first-come first-serve", and "overflow" can't be served. That's just a matter of basic resources - limits on personnel and time. So yes, it's possible that some people will get turned away if they see the schedule is completely filled.

As to wait time, it really depends on when you get there and pure luck. You can't call to find out how busy they are. A lot of people with appointments don't show up, but if they do then walk-ins need to wait behind them.

They do more than blood there, it's all body fluids, so wait time is not just dependent on whether you're getting a blood test or something else. If you really just need blood work, consider another an office that doesn't provide all of the other services too.

My personal experience today, Wednesday 9/28: I got in at 9:30AM, was called in at 9:40ish after they processed about 3 other people. The phlebotomist was done with me by 9:47. I had to give them urine and was out of the office by 9:55. I've had to wait longer in the past but I was still in and out within an hour. Working for myself I can get in while other people work 9-5 jobs. That's a huge factor which makes it more difficult for 9-5 workers and students but good for others like seniors.

As to quality and service. My contact was cordial and professional, efficient during the blood draw, conversational but not overly chatty. This was the best possible experience.

As a side note, there is a small street that goes around the parking lot and there is usually a space available, so it's free parking there if you can walk up a couple steps to get to the building. I don't know if they charge for parking in the lot but in my few visits I've never had to find out.

Everywhere we go we will find occasional delays and bad service, and we should report it in review places like this. But we should also balance the good experience reviews with the bad to see if a place has frequent problems or if there was just a bad day or two. Given my experiences which have been completely different from some others here, I'd say this place is fine with occasional common issues. For me a lot more bad reports would be needed for me to second-guess that impression.

I hope that helps others...</Review>

<user_id>107432612639662617077<//user_id>< username>
Anthony Minier<//username>
<date>1450274957386< /date><rating>4</rating>< text>
The name might suggest that this is primarily a burger joint and way way back when, it was. These days they still have some great burgers and an amazing chicken club sandwich along with onion rings and French fries. They have also added an extensive Mexican food menu as well. These guys know how to make some great Mexican dishes quickly too. There is only outdoor seating here but that area is covered to keep the rain off of you on those rare days that it rains in Southern California. Wear a jacket if it is chilly outside though because you will not be indoors at any time here. There is a walk up window where you place your order and another window where you will pick up your order once it is ready. Nothing here is prepared in advance. Your order is freshly cooked once you place it but these guys have mastered the art of quickly preparing any of their menu items so you won't be waiting too long for your food. The small wait is very much worth it. These are freshly made dishes done quickly but done right. I highly recommend their fish tacos or chicken club sandwich. Their chili cheese fries with freshly diced onions is a meal in itself and is a wonderful hangover cure. I quite honestly have never had anything from their menu that I did not like. There are also enough different choices that there is going to be something that will make your mouth and stomach happy you stopped by.< /text>

Quality Pet Stuff with a Local Touch.

Dexter's is a great little pet store in Del Mar village.  Our dogs love to visit because they always get treats. We are happy because of the quality of the treats and ingredients.

< Text>
Adorable little specialty pet store! Super clean, pet friendly, and every dog the customers bring in are so well-behaved. High quality brands with simple ingredient lists, affordable compared to other specialty pet stores and online, and their raw food variety actually blows my mind. Or rather, the variety they've squeezed into the little store does.

Dog Food:
‚Ä¢ Amazing variety of dog food, ranging from raw, freeze-dried, wet and dry.
‚Ä¢ Probably most known for their raw food.

Treats:
‚Ä¢ Usual pet store stuff like raw hide, bully sticks, dental chews, those popular Himalayan yak milk chews, fish skins, etc.
‚Ä¢ Doggy bakery goods and yogurts
‚Ä¢ Lots of freeze dried treats!

Supplements:
‚Ä¢ There is literally something for every doggy problem that occurs. Ranges from OTC dog medications to homeopathic/herbal.

Toys:
‚Ä¢ Smaller section that their food, but my God... they've selected at least a couple toys in every category of a dogs fetish...
¬∞ stuffingless, crinkle, squeek, plush, rubber, heavy chewers, thrashers, rope toys.. even replacement squeekers
‚Ä¢ Personal favorite: their self-branded red squeeky ball

Service:
‚Ä¢ The best. Extremely welcoming, helpful, knowledgeable and listens to every customer and their dogs.
‚Ä¢ They personally know everyone (and dog), and they always have treats and samples, which they're very generous with.

Everything I've bought here made me feel like it was worth every penny. They also have a loyalty program where you get $1 off every $25 you spend.</Text>

<Review>Don't be fooled by the name. ;) This is not a place to get your sandwiches. ;)
I first heard about this place when I was looking online for places that sold PrimalFoods (my dog's brand choice for dog food) close to my home in UTC.

Now, this is my pup's only grocery store. All of her meals and treats are purchased here.

FREQUENT BUYER CARD: This is the only store I know that sells the high-quality dog food along with other holistic/organic treats. There's also a WholeFoods down the street from me which is a lot closer that sells my dog's food, but Dexter's Deli's frequent buyer card program makes me come back here because I know I'll be saving money in the long run. It allows me to accumulate dollars with each purchase I make, and so when I have enough for a free bag of Primal Foods, I use it. ;) For Primal Foods, there's even a frequent buyer card for that that they've started just recently. So I'm saving a lot more!

STAFF:  The staff is very friendly and knows their products very well. A lot of repeat customers seem to walk in the store a lot, and the staff knows some of these people (and dogs!) by name. ;) Very nice to keep it all personal like that.

PARKING/LOCATION: If you are coming here for the first time, you might want to drive slow along Camino Del Mar because it can be easily missed. See some of the pictures here to get an idea of how the awning sign looks like. GPS can help, but even with GPS, I was close to missing it, and had to immediately pull in to the parking lot because I almost saw the sign too late. ;) Parking can be kinda tricky. The parking lot is small. There's probably only about 6 or 7 available parking spots to choose from, but some may or may not already be taken. It just depends what time of day you go. Pulling out from the parking lot can be a challenge if there are cars parked on the street. ;)

PRODUCTS: They sell healthy versions of all foods (for cats and dogs) dry and wet, (none of the commercial foods like Purina or Science Diet). They have really good treats (at least according to my dog they do), antler bones.... A section for grooming products (even the coveted Blueberry Facial wash!) cat toys, pet beds, pet clothes, socks, doggles, a whole shelf dedicated to dog toys, a small fresh bakery section (selling birthday cakes, cupcakes, etc), puzzle toys, dog music, leashes, collars, strollers, and other dog supplies.

ATMOSPHERE: A very "Del Mar" boutique vibe all throughout the store. Very friendly and laid-back. I have yet to bring my dog to this store, and then take a lazy stroll along Camino Del Mar. :) A lot of people during the weekends walking or biking along Camino Del Mar, and some even passing through here just to look around.<//Review>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<rate>5</rate><Text>Remarkably great Chinese cuisine, not just food.  Very fresh ingredients,clean-tasting sauces. Innovative use of shitaki and other mushrooms; delicious eggplant and tofu dishes; top quality chicken and beef, excellent vegetables such as green peppers, crisp bok choy, carrots, snow peas. Vegetarian egg rolls, sizzling rice soup, not greasy in any way. Great friendly enthusiastic and disciplined service from host Michael. Courteous takeout and prompt delivery. Surprising that such excellent food comes from this very clean but very plain space in a small strip mall; don't let the plain appearance fool you. Overlook the plain environment and location and focus on the food and you will have a fine dining experience. Amy's is my favorite over several "fine" Thai and Japanese restaurants in Sonoma County. Amy's isn't fancy, it's just plain good! If you're in the area, check it out!<//Text></record></dataset><record>
< userid>
106876508797523728408</userid>
<user_name>karen lee< /user_name><time>1484738281847</time><Rate>4< /Rate>< Text>
After living in Sonoma County for almost thirteen years I had given up hope of finding anything as good as what we get in San Francisco. I was thrilled to discover this gem right in my little town.

The food is prepard well, just the right amount of seasoning and each dish tastes just like it is supposed to rather than as if all the sauces came from the same bottle labeld "random brown sauce". The prices were very reasonable and the portions for take out were very generous.

Our order consisted of;
Ginger Beef; Perfect! Plenty of ginger, just delicious.
Combo Chow mein; loads of meat and vegies and just the right amount of sauce.
Mu Shu pork; The best I've had in years.
Braised Tofu with vegetables;I would have preferred it if the tofu was crispier, but it came with loads of vegetables.)

Amy's is officially my go to restaurant for chinese food.<//Text>
